# <a name="office-365-germany"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf086-104">Office 365 德国</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-104">Office 365 Germany</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf086-105">Office 365 德国是从欧洲可提供的 Office 365 服务中的一种区别选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-105">Office 365 Germany is a differentiated option from the Office 365 services already available across Europe.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-106">它通过在德国法律管辖的唯一数据受信者模型中提供了我们业界一流的数字工作工作效率服务（从德国数据中心起，通过 EFTA 中的数据访问和控制措施），帮助您满足德国最受管控客户的需求、欧盟 (EU) 和欧洲免费贸易协会 () 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-106">It helps address the needs of the most regulated customers in Germany, the European Union (EU), and the European Free Trade Association (EFTA) by delivering our industry-leading productivity services for digital work, from German data centers, with data residency in Germany and strict data access and control measures via a unique data trustee model governed under German law.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf086-p103">数据被信任方 T-Systems International 是一家独立的德国公司，同时也是德国电信的子公司，负责控制对客户数据的物理和逻辑访问。德国法律规定，未经数据被信任方的批准或监督，不能访问客户数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-p103">The data trustee, T-Systems International, an independent German company and subsidiary of Deutsche Telekom, controls physical and logical access to customer data. Customer data cannot be accessed without approval from or supervision by the data trustee, which is governed by German law.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf086-109">根据客户需求的这一发展，我们的云策略将重点放在德国与我们的全球云产品保持一致的新云区域的交付中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-109">Based on this evolution in customers' needs, our cloud strategy for Germany will focus on delivery of the new cloud regions in Germany that are consistent with our global cloud offering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-110">使用此焦点，我们将不再接受新客户或从当前可用的 Microsoft 云德国部署任何新服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-110">With this focus, we will no longer be accepting new customers or deploying any new services from the currently available Microsoft Cloud Germany.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-111">现有客户可以继续使用目前可用的云服务，我们将使用所需的安全更新进行维护。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-111">Existing customers can continue to use the current cloud services available today, which we'll maintain with necessary security updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-112">[了解 Office 365 德国](https://support.office.com/article/8a5a4bbc-667a-4cac-8769-d8ac9015db4c)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-112">[Learn about Office 365 Germany](https://support.office.com/article/8a5a4bbc-667a-4cac-8769-d8ac9015db4c).</span></span>

The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span><br><br>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-233"><sup>1</sup> 基于云的订阅服务，包括可在其中设置用户和域的 Microsoft 365 管理中心的相关功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-233"><sup>1</sup> Cloud-based subscription service with related features including the Microsoft 365 admin center where you can set up users and domains.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-234"><sup>2</sup> 可以分别购买 Office 365 ProPlus 计划。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-234"><sup>2</sup> You can buy an Office 365 ProPlus plan separately.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-235">Office 365 Germany 企业版 E3 和 Office 365 Germany 企业版 E4 中包含 Office 365 ProPlus。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-235">Office 365 ProPlus is included with Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 and Office 365 Germany Enterprise E4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-236">必须启用 [现代身份验证](https://support.office.com/article/modern-authentication-be-enabled-776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a)并与 Office 365 Germany 配合使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-236">[Modern authentication](https://support.office.com/article/modern-authentication-be-enabled-776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a) must be enabled for use with Office 365 Germany.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-237"><sup>3</sup> 虽然 Project Online 和 Power BI 不包括在内，但可以作为单独的附加服务进行购买，也可以免费添加到 Office 365 Germany 教育版 A1 计划中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-237"><sup>3</sup> Project Online and Power BI are not included, but can be purchased as a separate add-on service or added for free to the Office 365 Germany Education A1 plan.</span></span> <br/>

### <a name="what-compliance-certificates-are-provided-for-office-365-germany"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf086-246">为 Office 365 德国提供了哪些合规性证书？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-246">What compliance certificates are provided for Office 365 Germany?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1199"><sup>7</sup> The right to use client software applications, such as Office 365 ProPlus Office 2016, and Office 2013 is included in some Office 365 Germany plans.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1199"><sup>7</sup> The right to use client software applications, such as Office 365 ProPlus Office 2016, and Office 2013 is included in some Office 365 Germany plans.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1200">Client software applications run on an end user's device rather than in data centers in Germany.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1200">Client software applications run on an end user's device rather than in data centers in Germany.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1201">For purposes of your agreement with Microsoft, client software applications are not [German Online Services](https://microsoftvolumelicensing.com/DocumentSearch.aspx?Mode=3&amp;DocumentTypeId=58).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1201">For purposes of your agreement with Microsoft, client software applications are not [German Online Services](https://microsoftvolumelicensing.com/DocumentSearch.aspx?Mode=3&amp;DocumentTypeId=58).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1202">客户端软件应用程序也可能 lry 最终用户访问在线服务，而不是德语 Online 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1202">Client software applications also may lry an end user access online services that are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1203">German data residency commitments and access control by the German data trustee apply only to the German Online Services.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1203">German data residency commitments and access control by the German data trustee apply only to the German Online Services.</span></span><br/>

## <a name="office-application-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf086-1209">Office 应用程序功能  </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1209">Office application features</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1210">Office 365 Germany 计划包括在最终用户设备（"客户端软件应用程序"）上安装和运行的客户端软件应用程序，例如 Office 365 ProPlus、Office 2013\* 和 Office 2016。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1210">Office 365 Germany plans include client software applications that are installed and run on an end user's device ("client software applications"), such as Office 365 ProPlus, Office 2013\*, and Office 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1211">客户端软件应用程序不以独占方式在德国数据中心内运行，并且可能允许最终用户访问非 [德语 Online 服务](https://microsoftvolumelicensing.com/DocumentSearch.aspx?Mode=3&amp;DocumentTypeId=58)的联机服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1211">Client software applications do not operate exclusively in German data centers and may let an end user access online services that are not [German Online Services](https://microsoftvolumelicensing.com/DocumentSearch.aspx?Mode=3&amp;DocumentTypeId=58).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1212">鉴于你与 Microsoft 达成的协议，客户端软件应用程序不是 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1212">For purposes of your agreement with Microsoft, client software applications are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1213">德国数据驻留承诺和德国数据被信任方实施的访问控制只适用于 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1213">German data residency commitments and access control by German data trustee apply only to the German Online Services.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1214">\*适用于 Office 365 Germany 的 Office 2013 要求[启用新式验证](https://support.office.com/article/776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1214">\*Office 2013 for Office 365 Germany requires that [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1649"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 德国计划包括在最终用户的设备上安装和运行的客户端软件应用程序， ( "客户端软件应用程序" ) ，例如 Office 365 专业增强版、office 2013 和 office 2016。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1649"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 Germany plans include client software applications that are installed and run on an end-user's device ("client software applications"), such as Office 365 ProPlus, Office 2013, and Office 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1650">客户端软件应用程序不以独占方式在德国数据中心内运行，并且可能允许最终用户访问非德语 Online 服务的联机服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1650">Client software applications do not operate exclusively in German data centers and may let an end-user access online services that are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1651">鉴于你与 Microsoft 达成的协议，客户端软件应用程序不是 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1651">For purposes of your agreement with Microsoft, client software applications are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1652">德国数据驻留承诺和德国数据被信任方实施的访问控制只适用于 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1652">German data residency commitments and access control by German data trustee apply only to the German Online Services.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1653"><sup>2</sup> Office 2013 要求 [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1653"><sup>2</sup> Office 2013 requires that [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1654"><sup>3</sup> 不包含 Azure 信息保护，但可作为单独的附加项购买，以便启用支持的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1654"><sup>3</sup> Azure Information Protection is not included but can be purchased as a separate add-on in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-p118"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是一款本地服务器，必须进行单独购买和管理，才能启用支持的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-p118"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features. </span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1656"><sup>5</sup> 如果你拥有 Office Professional Plus 2013 或独立版 Excel 2013，可以下载并使用 [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=397382&amp;clcid=0x409)，将其作为不受支持的外接程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1656"><sup>5</sup> If you have Office Professional Plus 2013 or a standalone version of Excel 2013, you can download and use the [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=397382&amp;clcid=0x409) as an unsupported add-in.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1657"><sup>6</sup> Skype For business Basic 适用于所有客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1657"><sup>6</sup> Skype for Business Basic is available for all customers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1658">Skype for Business 桌面客户端是在本地安装的应用程序，为包含 Skype for Business Online 的 Office 365 计划提供状态、即时消息和会议功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1658">The Skype for Business desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1659">Office 365 ProPlus 和 Office 365 Germany 企业版 E3 包括完整的 Skype 应用程序，其中包含高级电话支持、存档及符合性功能等附加功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1659">Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 include the full Skype application, which includes additional features including advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1660">必须为每个用户分配 Skype for Business Online 许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1660">A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1661">有关 Lync 基本功能的详细信息，请参阅 [Dektop client comparison tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1661">For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Dektop client comparison tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1662"><sup>7</sup> 一些学校有资格享受教育增强版，其中包括 Office 365 ProPlus，并允许学生和教职员工在多达五个 PC 或 Mac 计算机上和其他移动设备（其中包括 Windows 平板电脑和 iPad）上安装最新版本的 Office。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1662"><sup>7</sup> Some schools are eligible for Education Plus, which includes Office 365 ProPlus, and allows students, faculty and staff to install the latest version of Office on up to five PC or Mac computers and on other mobile devices, including Windows tablets and the iPad.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1663">当通过订阅教育解决方案、开放式价值订阅教育解决方案或学校合同授权办公机构内的教职员工时，学校有资格使用 Office 365 教育增强版。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1663">Schools qualify for Office 365 Education Plus when they license Office institution-wide for faculty and staff through Enrollment for Education Solutions, Open Value Subscription Education Solutions, or a school contract.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1664">请注意，访问和发布服务器仅在电脑上可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1664">Note that Access and Publisher are available on PCs only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1665">OneNote for Mac 可从 Mac App Store 中单独下载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1665">OneNote for Mac is available as a separate download from the Mac App Store.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1666"><sup>8</sup> 可以安装但不可激活 Office 2011 for Mac。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1666"><sup>8</sup> Office 2011 for Mac can be installed, but not activated.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1667"><sup>9</sup> 批量激活 Office 365 Germany 企业版 E3，Office 365 ProPlus 仅限于安装在 Windows Server 2008 R2 和启用了 RDS 角色或安装了 Windows To Go 的更新版本上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1667"><sup>9</sup> Volume activation for Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 and Office 365 ProPlus is limited to installations on Windows Server 2008 R2 and newer with the RDS role enabled or Windows To Go installations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1668">在任一情况下，访问这些安装的用户应是 Office 365 Germany 企业版 E3 或 Office 365 ProPlus 许可的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1668">In either case, users accessing these installations need to be licensed users of Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 or Office 365 ProPlus.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1669">如果你在当前频道或延期频道的目标版本上，则当前提供<sup>10</sup>项访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1669"><sup>10</sup> Access is currently available if you're on Current Channel or on Targeted release for Deferred Channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1670">如果使用的是延期频道，则 Access 在 2017 年 6 月后可供使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1670">If you're on Deferred Channel, Access will be available in June 2017.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1671">有关详细信息，请参阅[包含在 Office 365 商业版和商业高级版中的 Access](https://support.office.com/article/f55c8362-5816-4f8b-897d-0a05e7ba0fef)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1671">For more information, see [Access included as part of Office 365 Business and Business Premium](https://support.office.com/article/f55c8362-5816-4f8b-897d-0a05e7ba0fef).</span></span><br/>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1866"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 德国计划包括在最终用户的设备上安装和运行的客户端软件应用程序， ( "客户端软件应用程序" ) ，例如 Office 365 专业增强版、office 2013 和 office 2016。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1866"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 Germany plans include client software applications that are installed and run on an end-user's device ("client software applications"), such as Office 365 ProPlus, Office 2013, and Office 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1867">客户端软件应用程序不以独占方式在德国数据中心内运行，并且可能允许最终用户访问非德语 Online 服务的联机服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1867">Client software applications do not operate exclusively in German data centers and may let an end-user access online services that are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1868">鉴于你与 Microsoft 达成的协议，客户端软件应用程序不是 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1868">For purposes of your agreement with Microsoft, client software applications are not German Online Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1869">德国数据驻留承诺和德国数据被信任方实施的访问控制只适用于 German Online Services。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1869">German data residency commitments and access control by German data trustee apply only to the German Online Services.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1870"><sup>2</sup> Office 2013 要求 [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1870"><sup>2</sup> Office 2013 requires that [modern authentication be enabled](https://support.office.com/article/776c0036-66fd-41cb-8928-5495c0f9168a).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1871"><sup>3</sup> 此版本的 Office 支持存档和合规性功能，但该功能未包含 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online 计划，且必须单独购买或与支持的等效本地服务器结合使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1871"><sup>3</sup> Archiving and compliance features are supported with this version of Office, but the Exchange Online and SharePoint Online plans are not included and must be purchased separately or used with supported on-premises server equivalents.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1872"><sup>4</sup> 不包含 Azure 信息保护，但可作为单独的附加项购买，以便启用支持的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1872"><sup>4</sup> Azure Information Protection is not included but can be purchased as a separate add-on in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1873"><sup>5</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是一款本地服务器，必须单独购买并管理，才能启用支持的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1873"><sup>5</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1874"><sup>6</sup> 如果你拥有 Office Professional Plus 2013 或独立版 Excel 2013，可以下载并使用 [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=397382&amp;clcid=0x409)，将其作为不受支持的外接程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1874"><sup>6</sup> If you have Office Professional Plus 2013 or a standalone version of Excel 2013, you can download and use the [Power Map Preview for Excel 2013](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=397382&amp;clcid=0x409) as an unsupported add-in.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1875"><sup>7</sup> Skype For business Basic 适用于所有客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1875"><sup>7</sup> Skype for Business Basic is available for all customers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1876">Skype for Business 桌面客户端是在本地安装的应用程序，为包含 Skype for Business Online 的 Office 365 计划提供状态、即时消息和会议功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1876">The Skype for Business desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1877">Office 365 ProPlus 和 Office 365 企业版 E3 包括完整的 Skype 应用程序，其中包含高级电话支持、存档及符合性功能等附加功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1877">Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Enterprise E3 include the full Skype application, which includes additional features including advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1878">必须为每个用户分配 Skype for Business Online 许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1878">A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1879">要详细了解 Lync Basic 功能，请参阅[桌面客户端比较表](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1879">For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Desktop client comparison tables](https://docs.microsoft.com/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1880"><sup>8</sup> 可以安装但不可激活 Office 2011 for Mac。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1880"><sup>8</sup> Office 2011 for Mac can be installed, but not activated.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1881"><sup>9</sup> Office 365 专业增强版在 (VDI) 的用户专用虚拟桌面基础结构上受支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1881"><sup>9</sup> Office 365 ProPlus is supported on user-dedicated virtual desktop infrastructure (VDI).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1882">通过批量许可计划进行购买时，Office 365 ProPlus 仅支持远程桌面服务 (RDS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1882">Office 365 ProPlus supports Remote Desktop Services (RDS) only when purchased through a Volume Licensing Program.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1883"><sup>10</sup> 批量激活 Office 365 Germany 企业版 E3，Office 365 ProPlus 仅限于安装在 Windows Server 2008 R2 和启用了 RDS 角色或安装了 Windows To Go 的更新版本上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1883"><sup>10</sup> Volume activation for Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 and Office 365 ProPlus is limited to installations on Windows Server 2008 R2 and newer with the RDS role enabled or Windows To Go installations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1884">在任一情况下，访问这些安装的用户应是 Office 365 Germany 企业版 E3 或 Office 365 ProPlus 许可的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1884">In either case, users accessing these installations need to be licensed users of Office 365 Germany Enterprise E3 or Office 365 ProPlus.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1885"><sup>11</sup> 不适用于 Office 365 Germany，但即将适用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1885"><sup>11</sup> Not available for Office 365 Germany, but coming soon.</span></span>

## <a name="office-for-the-web-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf086-1886">Office 网页版功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1886">Office for the web features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf086-1887">下表提供了 Office 365 德国的网站功能的比较的链接，这些功能在 Office 德国计划中提供的功能丰富的 Microsoft Office 桌面应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1887">The following table provides links to comparisons of Office for the web feature capabilities available in Office 365 Germany plans to feature-rich Microsoft Office desktop apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1888">使用比较来发现 Office for web 中可用的功能，然后选择功能名称，以阅读有关该功能如何工作的简短说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1888">Use the comparisons to discover what features are available in Office for the web and then select the feature name to read a brief description about how that feature works.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1889">您可能会发现组织中的某些人可能需要 Excel 桌面应用程序的高级图表功能，而其他人可能只需要查看和轻松地使用 Office for web 编辑 Word 文档和 PowerPoint 演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1889">You may discover that some people in your organization may need the advanced charting capability of the Excel desktop app while others may only need to view and lightly edit Word documents and PowerPoint presentations with Office for the web.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1890">仅选择了数量有限的 Office 功能来代表 Office 桌面套件的高级功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1890">A limited selection of Office features has been chosen to represent the advanced capabilities of the Office desktop suite.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1891">此表不是 Microsoft Office 2013 功能的完整列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1891">The table is not a comprehensive list of Microsoft Office features.</span></span> <br/>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1892">Microsoft Office 365 ProPlus 是最新 Office 桌面套件的按月订购产品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1892">Microsoft Office 365 ProPlus is a monthly subscription offer of the latest Office desktop suite.</span></span> <br/>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1893">如果 Microsoft Office Web Apps Server 2013 本地客户已购买 Office 桌面套件许可证（例如 Office Professional Plus、Office Standard 或 Office 365 专业增强版许可证），则可获得 Office 网页版编辑许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1893">Microsoft Office Web Apps Server 2013 on-premises customers get an Office for the web editing license if they have purchased an Office desktop suite license (such as Office Professional Plus, Office Standard, or an Office 365 ProPlus license).</span></span> <br/>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1894">由于 Office 365 德国的性质，某些功能尚未启用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1894">Due to the nature of Office 365 Germany, there are some features that have not yet been enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-1895">随着时间的推移，你将看到与全球服务一样，该服务功能会愈加健全。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-1895">You will see the services come closer to full feature parity with global services over time.</span></span>

## <a name="exchange-online-protection-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf086-2842">Exchange Online Protection 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2842">Exchange Online Protection features</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-2970"><sup>1</sup> 邮件用户被定义为"邮箱"，并且可以在 Exchange 管理中心 (EAC) 中与外部邮件联系人一起进行添加、删除或直接管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2970"><sup>1</sup> Mail users are defined as "Mailboxes," and, along with external mail contacts, can be added, removed, and otherwise managed directly in the Exchange admin center (EAC).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2971"><sup>2</sup>有 RBAC 自定义项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2971"><sup>2</sup> No RBAC customization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-2972">只有管理员角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2972">Admin roles only.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2973"><sup>3</sup>可在 EAC 中查看托管域和编辑域类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2973"><sup>3</sup> Managed domains can be viewed and domain types can be edited in the EAC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-2974">其他所有的域管理操作必须在 Microsoft 365 管理中心进行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2974">All other domain management must be done in the Microsoft 365 admin center.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2975"><sup>4</sup>有关 EOP 中的邮件流（也称为传输规则），请参阅 [Exchange Online 保护中的邮件流规则（传输规则）](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/mail-flow-rules-transport-rules-0)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2975"><sup>4</sup> Mail flow rules (also known as transport rules) in EOP are described in [Mail flow rules (transport rules) in Exchange Online Protection](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/mail-flow-rules-transport-rules-0).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-2976">EOP 与 Exchange Online 之间的可用邮件流规则条件、例外和操作有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2976">The available mail flow rule conditions, exceptions, and actions differ slightly between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-2977">有关这些区别，请参阅 [Exchange Online 中的邮件流规则条件和异常（谓词）](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions)和 [Exchange Online 中的邮件流规则](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2977">These differences are noted in [Mail flow rule conditions and exceptions (predicates) in Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions) and [Mail flow rule actions in Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2978"><sup>5</sup>EOP 审核报告是不包括邮箱信息的 Exchange Online 审核报告的子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2978"><sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2979"><sup>6</sup> DLP 策略提示不适用于 Exchange Enterprise CAL with Services 客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2979"><sup>6</sup> DLP policy tips are not available for Exchange Enterprise CAL with Services customers.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2980"><sup>7</sup> 默认内容筛选器操作旨在将垃圾邮件移到收件人的"垃圾邮件"文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2980"><sup>7</sup> The default content filter action is to move spam messages to the recipients' Junk Email folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-2981">要将此筛选器与本地 Exchange 邮箱结合使用，还需要在本地 Exchange 组织上配置两条传输规则，用于检测 EOP 添加的垃圾邮件头。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2981">For this to work with on-premises Exchange mailboxes, you also need to configure two transport rules in your on-premises Exchange organization to detect spam headers added by EOP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-2982">有关详细信息，请参阅 [确保垃圾邮件已路由到每个用户的"垃圾邮件"文件夹](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2982">For more information, see [Ensure that spam is routed to each user's Junk Email folder](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2983"><sup>8</sup> 此功能适用于将通过 EOP 筛选其邮箱的 Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) 客户，并且很快将提供给 Exchange Online 客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2983"><sup>8</sup> This feature is available to Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) customers whose mailboxes are being filtered by EOP, and will soon be available to Exchange Online customers.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2984"><sup>9</sup> EOP 审核报告是部分不包括邮箱信息的 Exchange Online 审核报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2984"><sup>9</sup> EOP reports are a subset of Exchange Online reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2985"><sup>10</sup> 包括 DLP 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2985"><sup>10</sup> Includes DLP reports.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2986"><sup>11</sup> Exchange Enterprise CAL with Services 客户应该通过选择 **Exchange Online** 服务（而不是 **Exchange Online Protection** 服务）来安装工作簿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2986"><sup>11</sup> Exchange Enterprise CAL with Services customers should install the workbook by selecting the **Exchange Online** service rather than the **Exchange Online Protection** service.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2987"><sup>12</sup> 支持购买 Azure 信息保护的本地客户，并使用 Exchange online Protection 通过 exchange online 路由电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2987"><sup>12</sup> Supported for on-premises customers who purchase Azure Information Protection and use Exchange Online Protection to route email through Exchange Online.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2988"><sup>13</sup> 扫描入站和出站邮件，但不扫描从组织中的发件人发送给组织中的收件人的内部邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2988"><sup>13</sup> Scans inbound and outbound messages, but does not scan internal messages sent from a sender in your organization to a recipient in your organization.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2989"><sup>14</sup> EOP 和 Exchange Online 的可用谓词和操作不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2989"><sup>14</sup> The available predicates and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2990"><sup>15</sup> 混合安装程序不能通过混合向导使用，但是，如果你拥有 Exchange SP1，则可以手动进行设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2990"><sup>15</sup> Hybrid setup is not available through the Hybrid Wizard, but can be set up manually if you have Exchange SP1.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2991"><sup>16</sup> 在 Office 365 德国 E1 及更高版本中可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2991"><sup>16</sup> Available in Office 365 Germany E1 and above.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2992"><sup>17</sup> 在 Office 365 德国 E3 中可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2992"><sup>17</sup> Available in Office 365 Germany E3.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-2993"><sup>18</sup> 适用于 Office 365 德国的附加功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-2993"><sup>18</sup> Available as an add-on feature for Office 365 Germany.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-5163"><sup>1</sup> 若要使用文件夹同步，您必须具有 office 2013 或更高版本 (Standard 或 Professional edition) 或包含 Office 应用程序的订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-5163"><sup>1</sup> To use folder sync, you must have Office 2013 or later (Standard or Professional edition) or a subscription that includes Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-5164">Office 365 Germany Business Essentials, Office 365 Germany Enterprise E1Office 365 Germany Enterprise E1, and Office 365 Germany Education A1 plans do not include subscriptions to Office desktop applications.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-5164">Office 365 Germany Business Essentials, Office 365 Germany Enterprise E1Office 365 Germany Enterprise E1, and Office 365 Germany Education A1 plans do not include subscriptions to Office desktop applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-5165">However, you can use folder sync if you have Office 2013 or later installed and subscribe to one of these plans.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-5165">However, you can use folder sync if you have Office 2013 or later installed and subscribe to one of these plans.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-5166"><sup>2</sup>Kiosk 帐户具有受限的 OneDrive for Business 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-5166"><sup>2</sup> Kiosk accounts have limited OneDrive for Business functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-5167">Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-5167">Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-5168">But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB of online storage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-5168">But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB of online storage.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-5169"><sup>3</sup> 不包含 Azure 信息保护，但可以作为单独的外接顺序购买，以启用支持的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-5169"><sup>3</sup> Azure Information Protection is not included, but can be purchased as a separate add-in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf086-5170">若要创建受 RMS 保护的内容，您必须具有 Office Professional 加上2013、Office Professional Plus 2016、Office 365 Pro Plus 或 Outlook Web Access。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-5170">To create RMS protected content you must have Office Professional Plus 2013, Office Professional Plus 2016, Office 365 Pro Plus, or Outlook Web Access.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="bf086-p157"><sup>4</sup>Kiosk 用户不能是管理员，因此包含 Kiosk 用户的租户至少必须有一个 Enterprise 用户才能访问管理中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf086-p157"><sup>4</sup> Because Kiosk users can't be administrators, tenants with Kiosk users need at least one Enterprise user to access the admin center. </span></span><br/>
